2→\"\"\"\n     3→Evaluation script for truth_analysis probing task.\n     4→Validates the agent's probe and computes metrics.\n     5→\"\"\"\n     6→import argparse\n     7→import json\n     8→import pickle\n     9→from pathlib import Path\n    10→import numpy as np\n    11→from sklearn.metrics import (\n    12→    accuracy_score,\n    13→    precision_recall_fscore_support,\n    14→    roc_auc_score,\n    15→    classification_report\n    16→)\n    17→import torch\n    18→from transformers import AutoModel, AutoTokenizer\n    19→\n    20→\n    21→def load_labeled_data(data_file, behavioral_labels_file=None):\n    22→    \"\"\"Load labeled data, preferring behavioral_labels.jsonl if it exists.\"\"\"\n    23→    source = behavioral_labels_file if (behavioral_labels_file and Path(behavioral_labels_file).exists()) else data_file\n    24→    print(f\"Loading labels from: {source}\")\n    25→    texts, labels = [], []\n    26→    with open(source, 'r') as f:\n    27→        for line in f:\n    28→            item = json.loads(line)\n    29→            texts.append(item['text'])\n    30→            labels.append(item['label'])\n    31→    return texts, np.array(labels)\n    32→\n    33→\n    34→def extract_activations(model, tokenizer, texts, layer_idx=-1, aggregation='mean'):\n    35→    \"\"\"\n    36→    Extract activations from specified layer.\n    37→\n    38→    Args:\n    39→        model: HuggingFace model\n    40→        tokenizer: HuggingFace tokenizer\n    41→        texts: List of text strings\n    42→        layer_idx: Layer index (-1 for last layer)\n    43→        aggregation: Token aggregation method ('first', 'last', 'mean', 'max')\n    44→    \"\"\"\n    45→    model.eval()\n    46→    activations = []\n    47→\n    48→    with torch.no_grad():\n    49→        for text in texts:\n    50→            inputs = tokenizer(text, return_tensors=\"pt\", truncation=True, max_length=512)\n    51→\n    52→            # Move to GPU if available\n    53→            if torch.cuda.is_available():\n    54→                inputs = {k: v.cuda() for k, v in inputs.items()}\n    55→                model = model.cuda()\n    56→\n    57→            outputs = model(**inputs, output_hidden_states=True)\n    58→            hidden_states = outputs.hidden_states[layer_idx].cpu().numpy()  # (1, seq_len, hidden_dim)\n    59→\n    60→            # Aggregate tokens\n    61→            if aggregation == 'first':\n    62→                act = hidden_states[0, 0, :]  # First token\n    63→            elif aggregation == 'last':\n    64→ HuggingFace model\n        tokenizer: HuggingFace tokenizer\n        texts: List of text strings\n        layer_idx: Layer index (-1 for last layer)\n        aggregation: Token aggregation method ('first', 'last', 'mean', 'max')\n    \"\"\"\n    model.eval()\n    activations = []\n\n    with torch.no_grad():\n        for text in texts:\n            inputs = tokenizer(text, (1, seq_len, hidden_dim)\n\n            # Aggregate tokens\n            if aggregation == 'first':\n                act = hidden_states[0, 0, :]  # First token\n            elif aggregation == aggregation = probe_data.get('aggregation', 'mean') if isinstance(probe_data, dict) else 'mean'\n\n    scaler = probe_data.get('scaler') if isinstance(probe_data, dict) else None\n    if scaler is not args.json_output_file:\n            with open(args.json_output_file, 'w') as f:\n                json.dump(metrics, f, indent=2)\n        return\n\n    # Load probe\n    print(f\"Loading probe from: Remove common prefixes\n    for prefix in [\"the answer is\", \"answer:\", \"a:\", \"i think\", \"i believe\"]:\n        if text.startswith(prefix):\n            text = text[len(prefix):].strip()\n    # Remove punctuation\n    text = text.translate(str.maketrans('', '', string.punctuation))\n    # Normalize whitespace\n    text = ' '.join(text.split())\n    return text\n\ndef check_answer_match(model_response, correct_answers):\n    \"\"\"\n    Check if model response matches any correct answer.\n    Uses multiple matching strategies.\n    \"\"\"\n    response_norm = normalize_text(model_response)\n\n    for correct in correct_answers:\n        correct_norm = normalize_text(correct)\n\n        # Direct containment check (either direction)\n        if correct_norm in response_norm or response_norm in correct_norm:\n            return True\n\n        # Check key phrases from correct answer\n        # Extract meaningful words (longer than 3 chars)\n        correct_words = set(correct_norm.split())\n        response_words = set(response_norm.split())\n\n        # Remove common stop words\n        stop_words = {'the', 'a', 'an', 'is', 'are', 'was', 'were', 'be', 'been',\n                      'being', 'have', 'has', 'had', 'do', 'does', 'did', 'will',\n                      'would', 'could', 'should', 'may', 'might', 'can', 'shall',\n                      'that', 'this', 'these', 'those', 'and', 'but', 'or', 'nor',\n                      'not', 'no', 'yes', 'for', 'of', 'in', 'on', 'at', 'to',\n                      'from', 'by', 'with', 'as', 'its', 'it', 'he', 'she', 'they',\n                      'we', 'you', 'i', 'me', 'my', 'your', 'his', 'her', 'our',\n                      'their', 'what', 'which', 'who', 'whom', 'how', 'when', 'where',\n                      'why', 'if', 'then', 'than', 'so', 'just', 'about', 'up', 'out',\n                      'into', 'over', 'after', 'before', 'between', 'under', 'again'}\n\n        correct_key = correct_words - stop_words\n        response_key = response_words - stop_words\n\n        if len(correct_key) > 0:\n            overlap = correct_key & response_key\n            overlap_ratio = len(overlap) / len(correct_key)\n            if overlap_ratio >= 0.6:\n                return True\n\n    return False\n\ndef main():\n    print(\"Loading model and tokenizer...\")\n    model_name = \"HuggingFaceTB/SmolLM2-1.7B\"\n    tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained(model_name)\n    model = AutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained(model_name, torch_dtype=torch.float16)\n\n    if torch.cuda.is_available():\n        model = model.cuda()\n    model.eval()\n\n    # Set pad token\n    if tokenizer.pad_token is None:\n        tokenizer.pad_token = tokenizer.eos_token\n\n    # Load data\n    print(\"Loading questions...\")\n    data = []\n    with open(\"labeled_data.jsonl\", \"r\") as f:\n        for line in f:\n            data.append(json.loads(line))\n\n    print(f\"Total questions: {len(data)}\")\n\n    # Generate responses and label\n    results = []\n    correct_count = 0\n\n    for i, item in enumerate(data):\n        question = item[\"text\"]\n        correct_answers = item[\"correct_answers\"]\n\n        # Format prompt - simple Q&A format\n        prompt = f\"Q: {question}\\nA:\"\n\n        inputs = tokenizer(prompt, return_tensors=\"pt\", truncation=True, max_length=256)\n        if torch.cuda.is_available():\n            inputs = {k: v.cuda() for k, v in inputs.items()}\n\n        with torch.no_grad():\n            outputs = model.generate(\n                **inputs,\n                max_new_tokens=100,\n                do_sample=False,\n                temperature=1.0,\n                pad_token_id=tokenizer.eos_token_id,\n            )\n\n        # Decode only the generated part\n        input_len = inputs[\"input_ids\"].shape[1]\n        response = tokenizer.decode(outputs[0][input_len:], skip_special_tokens=True).strip()\n\n        # Take only first sentence/line\n        response_first = response.split('\\n')[0].strip()\n        if '.' in response_first:\n            response_first = response_first.split('.')[0] + '.'\n\n        # Check if correct\n        is_correct = check_answer_match(response, correct_answers)\n        label = 1 if is_correct else 0\n        correct_count += label\n\n        results.append({\n            \"text\": question,\n            \"label\": label,\n            \"model_response\": response_first,\n            \"correct_answers\": correct_answers\n        })\n\n        if (i + 1) % 50 == 0:\n            print(f\"  [{i+1}/{len(data)}] Correct so far: {correct_count}/{i+1} ({correct_count/(i+1)*100:.1f}%)\")\n\n    print(f\"\\nFinal: {correct_count}/{len(data)} correct ({correct_count/len(data)*100:.1f}%)\")\n\n    # Save behavioral labels\n    with open(\"behavioral_labels.jsonl\", \"w\") as f:\n        for r in results:\n            f.write(json.dumps({\"text\": r[\"text\"], \"label\": r[\"label\"]}) + \"\\n\")\n\n    # Save detailed results for debugging\n    with open(\"behavioral_labels_detailed.jsonl\", \"w\") as f:\n        for r in results:\n            f.write(json.dumps(r) + \"\\n\")\n\n    print(f\"Saved behavioral labels to behavioral_labels.jsonl\")\n\n    # Print some examples\n    print(\"\\n--- Example correct answers ---\")\n    correct_examples = [r for r in results if r[\"label\"] == 1][:5]\n    for ex in correct_examples:\n        print(f\"  Q: {ex['text']}\")\n        print(f\"  Model: {ex['model_response']}\")\n        print()\n\n    print(\"--- Example incorrect answers ---\")\n    incorrect_examples = [r for r in results if r[\"label\"] == 0][:5]\n    for ex in incorrect_examples:\n        print(f\"  Q: {ex['text']}\")\n        print(f\"  Model: {ex['model_response']}\")\n        print(f\"  Correct: {ex['correct_answers'][:2]}\")\n        print()\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"stop_details":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":393,"cache_read_input_tokens":24590,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":393,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"global"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"f0cda53f-9198-46c2-b0ae-9e4a0de1b490","uuid":"ca4d43ee-70ac-4b9d-9bb6-4896fe959f08"}

[2026-06-10 11:30:41 UTC] {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-opus-4-6","id":"msg_01Ps1H1LpThkt6NpgoDEEJAS","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01FRJ4iQEinTMrkkqojqkVhj","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/iopsstor/scratch/cscs/oyasunaga/autointerp_runs/jobs/truth_analysis_HuggingFaceTB_SmolLM2-1.7B_2513490/run_probing.py","content":"#!/usr/bin/env python3\n\"\"\"\nFull probing pipeline for truth analysis:\n1. Extract activations from all layers\n2. Train linear probes with cross-validation\n3. Test different token aggregation strategies\n4. Generate metrics and visualizations\n5. Save best probe\n\"\"\"\nimport json\nimport pickle\nimport os\nimport numpy as np\nimport torch\nfrom transformers import AutoModel, AutoTokenizer\nfrom sklearn.linear_model import LogisticRegression\nfrom sklearn.model_selection import StratifiedKFold\nfrom sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler\nfrom sklearn.metrics import (\n    accuracy_score, precision_recall_fscore_support,\n    roc_auc_score, classification_report\n)\nimport matplotlib\nmatplotlib.use('Agg')\nimport matplotlib.pyplot as plt\nfrom pathlib import Path\nimport time\n\ndef load_behavioral_labels(filepath=\"behavioral_labels.jsonl\"):\n    texts, labels = [], []\n    with open(filepath, 'r') as f:\n        for line in f:\n            item = json.loads(line)\n            texts.append(item['text'])\n            labels.append(item['label'])\n    return texts, np.array(labels)\n\ndef extract_all_activations(model, tokenizer, texts, batch_size=16):\n    \"\"\"Extract activations from ALL layers for all texts.\"\"\"\n    model.eval()\n    device = next(model.parameters()).device\n    num_layers = model.config.num_hidden_layers + 1  # +1 for embedding layer\n\n    # Store activations for each layer\n    all_activations = {\n        'first': [[] for _ in range(num_layers)],\n        'last': [[] for _ in range(num_layers)],\n        'mean': [[] for _ in range(num_layers)],\n        'max': [[] for _ in range(num_layers)],\n    }\n\n    with torch.no_grad():\n        for i in range(0, len(texts), batch_size):\n            batch_texts = texts[i:i+batch_size]\n\n            inputs = tokenizer(\n                batch_texts, return_tensors=\"pt\",\n                truncation=True, max_length=512,\n                padding=True\n            )\n            inputs = {k: v.to(device) for k, v in inputs.items()}\n\n            outputs = model(**inputs, output_hidden_states=True)\n            hidden_states = outputs.hidden_states  # tuple of (batch, seq_len, hidden_dim)\n\n            attention_mask = inputs.get('attention_mask', None)\n\n            for layer_idx in range(num_layers):\n                hs = hidden_states[layer_idx].cpu().float().numpy()  # (batch, seq_len, hidden)\n\n                for b in range(hs.shape[0]):\n                    if attention_mask is not None:\n                        mask = attention_mask[b].cpu().numpy()\n                        seq_len = int(mask.sum())\n                    else:\n                        seq_len = hs.shape[1]\n\n                    # First token\n                    all_activations['first'][layer_idx].append(hs[b, 0, :])\n\n                    # Last token (last non-padding token)\n                    all_activations['last'][layer_idx].append(hs[b, seq_len-1, :])\n\n                    # Mean pooling (over non-padding tokens)\n                    all_activations['mean'][layer_idx].append(hs[b, :seq_len, :].mean(axis=0))\n\n                    # Max pooling (over non-padding tokens)\n                    all_activations['max'][layer_idx].append(hs[b, :seq_len, :].max(axis=0))\n\n            if (i + batch_size) % 100 == 0 or i + batch_size >= len(texts):\n                print(f\"  Extracted {min(i+batch_size, len(texts))}/{len(texts)}\")\n\n    # Convert to numpy arrays\n    for agg in all_activations:\n        for layer_idx in range(num_layers):\n            all_activations[agg][layer_idx] = np.array(all_activations[agg][layer_idx])\n\n    return all_activations\n\ndef train_probe_cv(X, y, n_folds=5, C=1.0):\n    \"\"\"Train a logistic regression probe with cross-validation.\"\"\"\n    skf = StratifiedKFold(n_splits=n_folds, shuffle=True, random_state=42)\n\n    accuracies = []\n    precisions = []\n    recalls = []\n    f1s = []\n    aucs = []\n\n    for fold, (train_idx, val_idx) in enumerate(skf.split(X, y)):\n        X_train, X_val = X[train_idx], X[val_idx]\n        y_train, y_val = y[train_idx], y[val_idx]\n\n        scaler = StandardScaler()\n        X_train_s = scaler.fit_transform(X_train)\n        X_val_s = scaler.transform(X_val)\n\n        probe = LogisticRegression(C=C, max_iter=1000, random_state=42, solver='lbfgs')\n        probe.fit(X_train_s, y_train)\n\n        y_pred = probe.predict(X_val_s)\n        y_proba = probe.predict_proba(X_val_s)[:, 1]\n\n        accuracies.append(accuracy_score(y_val, y_pred))\n        p, r, f, _ = precision_recall_fscore_support(y_val, y_pred, average='binary', zero_division=0)\n        precisions.append(p)\n        recalls.append(r)\n        f1s.append(f)\n        try:\n            aucs.append(roc_auc_score(y_val, y_proba))\n        except:\n            aucs.append(0.5)\n\n    return {\n        'accuracy': np.mean(accuracies),\n        'accuracy_std': np.std(accuracies),\n        'precision': np.mean(precisions),\n        'recall': np.mean(recalls),\n        'f1': np.mean(f1s),\n        'roc_auc': np.mean(aucs),\n        'roc_auc_std': np.std(aucs),\n    }\n\ndef main():\n    start_time = time.time()\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n    print(\"Truth Analysis Probing Pipeline\")\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n\n    # Load data\n    print(\"\\n1. Loading behavioral labels...\")\n    texts, labels = load_behavioral_labels()\n    print(f\"   Loaded {len(texts)} examples\")\n    print(f\"   Label distribution: {np.sum(labels==1)} correct (1), {np.sum(labels==0)} incorrect (0)\")\n    print(f\"   Baseline accuracy (majority class): {max(np.mean(labels), 1-np.mean(labels)):.3f}\")\n\n    # Load model\n    print(\"\\n2. Loading model...\")\n    model_name = \"HuggingFaceTB/SmolLM2-1.7B\"\n    tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained(model_name)\n    model = AutoModel.from_pretrained(model_name, torch_dtype=torch.float16)\n\n    if tokenizer.pad_token is None:\n        tokenizer.pad_token = tokenizer.eos_token\n\n    if torch.cuda.is_available():\n        model = model.cuda()\n    model.eval()\n\n    num_layers = model.config.num_hidden_layers + 1\n    print(f\"   Model loaded: {num_layers} layers (including embedding), hidden_size={model.config.hidden_size}\")\n\n    # Extract activations\n    print(\"\\n3. Extracting activations from all layers...\")\n    activations = extract_all_activations(model, tokenizer, texts, batch_size=8)\n    print(f\"   Done! Shape check - layer 0, mean: {activations['mean'][0].shape}\")\n\n    # Free model memory\n    del model\n    torch.cuda.empty_cache()\n\n    # Train probes\n    print(\"\\n4. Training probes across all layers and aggregation strategies...\")\n    aggregation_methods = ['first', 'last', 'mean', 'max']\n    results = {}\n\n    best_score = -1\n    best_config = None\n    best_X = None\n\n    for agg in aggregation_methods:\n        results[agg] = []\n        print(f\"\\n   --- Aggregation: {agg} ---\")\n        for layer_idx in range(num_layers):\n            X = activations[agg][layer_idx]\n            metrics = train_probe_cv(X, labels, n_folds=5)\n            metrics['layer'] = layer_idx\n            metrics['aggregation'] = agg\n            results[agg].append(metrics)\n\n            if metrics['roc_auc'] > best_score:\n                best_score = metrics['roc_auc']\n                best_config = (agg, layer_idx)\n                best_X = X.copy()\n\n            if layer_idx % 6 == 0 or layer_idx == num_layers - 1:\n                print(f\"   Layer {layer_idx:2d}: Acc={metrics['accuracy']:.3f} (±{metrics['accuracy_std']:.3f}), \"\n                      f\"F1={metrics['f1']:.3f}, AUC={metrics['roc_auc']:.3f} (±{metrics['roc_auc_std']:.3f})\")\n\n    print(f\"\\n   Best config: {best_config[0]} aggregation, layer {best_config[1]} \"\n          f\"(AUC={best_score:.3f})\")\n\n    # Train final probe on best config\n    print(\"\\n5. Training final probe on best configuration...\")\n    best_agg, best_layer = best_config\n\n    scaler = StandardScaler()\n    X_scaled = scaler.fit_transform(best_X)\n\n    # Try different regularization strengths\n    best_C = 1.0\n    best_C_score = -1\n    for C in [0.01, 0.1, 1.0, 10.0]:\n        cv_metrics = train_probe_cv(best_X, labels, n_folds=5, C=C)\n        print(f\"   C={C}: AUC={cv_metrics['roc_auc']:.3f}, Acc={cv_metrics['accuracy']:.3f}\")\n        if cv_metrics['roc_auc'] > best_C_score:\n            best_C_score = cv_metrics['roc_auc']\n            best_C = C\n\n    print(f\"   Best C: {best_C} (AUC={best_C_score:.3f})\")\n\n    # Train final model on all data\n    final_probe = LogisticRegression(C=best_C, max_iter=1000, random_state=42, solver='lbfgs')\n    final_probe.fit(X_scaled, labels)\n\n    # Save probe\n    os.makedirs(\"final_probe\", exist_ok=True)\n    probe_data = {\n        'model': final_probe,\n        'scaler': scaler,\n        'layer': best_layer,\n        'aggregation': best_agg,\n        'C': best_C,\n        'num_layers': num_layers,\n        'hidden_size': best_X.shape[1],\n    }\n    with open(\"final_probe/probe.pkl\", \"wb\") as f:\n        pickle.dump(probe_data, f)\n    print(f\"   Saved probe to final_probe/probe.pkl\")\n\n    # Get final metrics via cross-validation\n    final_cv_metrics = train_probe_cv(best_X, labels, n_folds=5, C=best_C)\n\n    # Also compute full-data metrics\n    y_pred_full = final_probe.predict(X_scaled)\n    y_proba_full = final_probe.predict_proba(X_scaled)[:, 1]\n    full_acc = accuracy_score(labels, y_pred_full)\n    full_p, full_r, full_f1, _ = precision_recall_fscore_support(labels, y_pred_full, average='binary')\n    full_auc = roc_auc_score(labels, y_proba_full)\n\n    metrics_output = {\n        'best_layer': int(best_layer),\n        'best_aggregation': best_agg,\n        'best_C': float(best_C),\n        'cv_accuracy': float(final_cv_metrics['accuracy']),\n        'cv_accuracy_std': float(final_cv_metrics['accuracy_std']),\n        'cv_precision': float(final_cv_metrics['precision']),\n        'cv_recall': float(final_cv_metrics['recall']),\n        'cv_f1': float(final_cv_metrics['f1']),\n        'cv_roc_auc': float(final_cv_metrics['roc_auc']),\n        'cv_roc_auc_std': float(final_cv_metrics['roc_auc_std']),\n        'train_accuracy': float(full_acc),\n        'train_precision': float(full_p),\n        'train_recall': float(full_r),\n        'train_f1': float(full_f1),\n        'train_roc_auc': float(full_auc),\n        'num_examples': int(len(labels)),\n        'num_positive': int(np.sum(labels == 1)),\n        'num_negative': int(np.sum(labels == 0)),\n        'baseline_accuracy': float(max(np.mean(labels), 1 - np.mean(labels))),\n    }\n\n    with open(\"metrics.json\", \"w\") as f:\n        json.dump(metrics_output, f, indent=2)\n    print(f\"   Saved metrics to metrics.json\")\n\n    # 6. Generate Visualizations\n    print(\"\\n6. Generating visualizations...\")\n\n    # Plot 1: Probe accuracy across layers for all aggregation methods\n    fig, axes = plt.subplots(2, 2, figsize=(14, 10))\n\n    # Accuracy across layers\n    ax = axes[0, 0]\n    for agg in aggregation_methods:\n        layers = [r['layer'] for r in results[agg]]\n        accs = [r['accuracy'] for r in results[agg]]\n        ax.plot(layers, accs, marker='o', label=agg, linewidth=2, markersize=4)\n    ax.axhline(y=max(np.mean(labels), 1-np.mean(labels)), color='gray', linestyle='--', label='baseline', alpha=0.7)\n    ax.set_xlabel('Layer')\n    ax.set_ylabel('Accuracy')\n    ax.set_title('Probe Accuracy Across Layers')\n    ax.legend()\n    ax.grid(True, alpha=0.3)\n\n    # ROC-AUC across layers\n    ax = axes[0, 1]\n    for agg in aggregation_methods:\n        layers = [r['layer'] for r in results[agg]]\n        aucs = [r['roc_auc'] for r in results[agg]]\n        ax.plot(layers, aucs, marker='o', label=agg, linewidth=2, markersize=4)\n    ax.axhline(y=0.5, color='gray', linestyle='--', label='chance', alpha=0.7)\n    ax.set_xlabel('Layer')\n    ax.set_ylabel('ROC-AUC')\n    ax.set_title('Probe ROC-AUC Across Layers')\n    ax.legend()\n    ax.grid(True, alpha=0.3)\n\n    # F1 across layers\n    ax = axes[1, 0]\n    for agg in aggregation_methods:\n        layers = [r['layer'] for r in results[agg]]\n        f1s = [r['f1'] for r in results[agg]]\n        ax.plot(layers, f1s, marker='o', label=agg, linewidth=2, markersize=4)\n    ax.set_xlabel('Layer')\n    ax.set_ylabel('F1 Score')\n    ax.set_title('Probe F1 Score Across Layers')\n    ax.legend()\n    ax.grid(True, alpha=0.3)\n\n    # Best aggregation comparison (bar chart)\n    ax = axes[1, 1]\n    best_auc_per_agg = {}\n    for agg in aggregation_methods:\n        aucs = [r['roc_auc'] for r in results[agg]]\n        best_idx = np.argmax(aucs)\n        best_auc_per_agg[agg] = {\n            'auc': aucs[best_idx],\n            'layer': best_idx,\n            'acc': results[agg][best_idx]['accuracy'],\n            'f1': results[agg][best_idx]['f1'],\n        }\n\n    x_pos = range(len(aggregation_methods))\n    bars_auc = [best_auc_per_agg[agg]['auc'] for agg in aggregation_methods]\n    bars_acc = [best_auc_per_agg[agg]['acc'] for agg in aggregation_methods]\n    bars_f1 = [best_auc_per_agg[agg]['f1'] for agg in aggregation_methods]\n\n    width = 0.25\n    ax.bar([x - width for x in x_pos], bars_auc, width, label='ROC-AUC', alpha=0.8)\n    ax.bar(list(x_pos), bars_acc, width, label='Accuracy', alpha=0.8)\n    ax.bar([x + width for x in x_pos], bars_f1, width, label='F1', alpha=0.8)\n    ax.set_xticks(list(x_pos))\n    labels_agg = [f\"{agg}\\n(L{best_auc_per_agg[agg]['layer']})\" for agg in aggregation_methods]\n    ax.set_xticklabels(labels_agg)\n    ax.set_ylabel('Score')\n    ax.set_title('Best Performance per Aggregation Strategy')\n    ax.legend()\n    ax.grid(True, alpha=0.3, axis='y')\n\n    plt.suptitle('Truth Analysis Probing: SmolLM2-1.7B on TruthfulQA', fontsize=14, fontweight='bold')\n    plt.tight_layout()\n    plt.savefig('probe_performance_layers.png', dpi=150, bbox_inches='tight')\n    plt.close()\n    print(\"   Saved probe_performance_layers.png\")\n\n    # Plot 2: Heatmap of AUC across layers and aggregations\n    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(10, 6))\n    auc_matrix = np.zeros((len(aggregation_methods), num_layers))\n    for i, agg in enumerate(aggregation_methods):\n        for j in range(num_layers):\n            auc_matrix[i, j] = results[agg][j]['roc_auc']\n\n    im = ax.imshow(auc_matrix, aspect='auto', cmap='YlOrRd', interpolation='nearest')\n    ax.set_yticks(range(len(aggregation_methods)))\n    ax.set_yticklabels(aggregation_methods)\n    ax.set_xlabel('Layer')\n    ax.set_ylabel('Aggregation')\n    ax.set_title('ROC-AUC Heatmap: Layer x Aggregation')\n    plt.colorbar(im, ax=ax, label='ROC-AUC')\n\n    # Annotate\n    for i in range(len(aggregation_methods)):\n        for j in range(num_layers):\n            val = auc_matrix[i, j]\n            color = 'white' if val > 0.6 else 'black'\n            ax.text(j, i, f'{val:.2f}', ha='center', va='center', fontsize=6, color=color)\n\n    plt.tight_layout()\n    plt.savefig('probe_heatmap.png', dpi=150, bbox_inches='tight')\n    plt.close()\n    print(\"   Saved probe_heatmap.png\")\n\n    # Plot 3: Accuracy with error bars for best aggregation\n    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(10, 5))\n    layers = range(num_layers)\n    accs = [results[best_agg][l]['accuracy'] for l in layers]\n    stds = [results[best_agg][l]['accuracy_std'] for l in layers]\n    aucs_best = [results[best_agg][l]['roc_auc'] for l in layers]\n    auc_stds = [results[best_agg][l]['roc_auc_std'] for l in layers]\n\n    ax.errorbar(list(layers), accs, yerr=stds, marker='o', linewidth=2, markersize=5,\n                capsize=3, label=f'Accuracy ({best_agg})', color='tab:blue')\n    ax.errorbar(list(layers), aucs_best, yerr=auc_stds, marker='s', linewidth=2, markersize=5,\n                capsize=3, label=f'ROC-AUC ({best_agg})', color='tab:red')\n    ax.axhline(y=max(np.mean(labels), 1-np.mean(labels)), color='gray', linestyle='--',\n               label='Baseline accuracy', alpha=0.7)\n    ax.axhline(y=0.5, color='lightgray', linestyle=':', label='Chance AUC', alpha=0.7)\n    ax.set_xlabel('Layer')\n    ax.set_ylabel('Score')\n    ax.set_title(f'Probe Performance with Confidence (Best Aggregation: {best_agg})')\n    ax.legend()\n    ax.grid(True, alpha=0.3)\n    plt.tight_layout()\n    plt.savefig('probe_confidence.png', dpi=150, bbox_inches='tight')\n    plt.close()\n    print(\"   Saved probe_confidence.png\")\n\n    # [2026-06-10 11:30:41 UTC] {"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01FRJ4iQEinTMrkkqojqkVhj","type":"tool_result","content":"File created successfully at: /iopsstor/scratch/cscs/oyasunaga/autointerp_runs/jobs/truth_analysis_HuggingFaceTB_SmolLM2-1.7B_2513490/run_probing.py"}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"f0cda53f-9198-46c2-b0ae-9e4a0de1b490","uuid":"7df73756-67ab-473c-ac00-596aa4bcb707","tool_use_result":{"type":"create","filePath":"/iopsstor/scratch/cscs/oyasunaga/autointerp_runs/jobs/truth_analysis_HuggingFaceTB_SmolLM2-1.7B_2513490/run_probing.py","content":"#!/usr/bin/env python3\n\"\"\"\nFull probing pipeline for truth analysis:\n1. Extract activations from all layers\n2. Train linear probes with cross-validation\n3. Test different token aggregation strategies\n4. Generate metrics and visualizations\n5. Save best probe\n\"\"\"\nimport json\nimport pickle\nimport os\nimport numpy as np\nimport torch\nfrom transformers import AutoModel, AutoTokenizer\nfrom sklearn.linear_model import LogisticRegression\nfrom sklearn.model_selection import StratifiedKFold\nfrom sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler\nfrom sklearn.metrics import (\n    accuracy_score, precision_recall_fscore_support,\n    roc_auc_score, classification_report\n)\nimport matplotlib\nmatplotlib.use('Agg')\nimport matplotlib.pyplot as plt\nfrom pathlib import Path\nimport time\n\ndef load_behavioral_labels(filepath=\"behavioral_labels.jsonl\"):\n    texts, labels = [], []\n    with open(filepath, 'r') as f:\n        for line in f:\n            item = json.loads(line)\n            texts.append(item['text'])\n            labels.append(item['label'])\n    return texts, np.array(labels)\n\ndef extract_all_activations(model, tokenizer, texts, batch_size=16):\n    \"\"\"Extract activations from ALL layers for all texts.\"\"\"\n    model.eval()\n    device = next(model.parameters()).device\n    num_layers = model.config.num_hidden_layers + 1  # +1 for embedding layer\n\n    # Store activations for each layer\n    all_activations = {\n        'first': [[] for _ in range(num_layers)],\n        'last': [[] for _ in range(num_layers)],\n        'mean': [[] for _ in range(num_layers)],\n        'max': [[] for _ in range(num_layers)],\n    }\n\n    with torch.no_grad():\n        for i in range(0, len(texts), batch_size):\n            batch_texts = texts[i:i+batch_size]\n\n            inputs = tokenizer(\n                batch_texts, return_tensors=\"pt\",\n                truncation=True, max_length=512,\n                padding=True\n            )\n            inputs = {k: v.to(device) for k, v in inputs.items()}\n\n            outputs = model(**inputs, output_hidden_states=True)\n            hidden_states = outputs.hidden_states  # tuple of (batch, seq_len, hidden_dim)\n\n            attention_mask = inputs.get('attention_mask', None)\n\n            for layer_idx in range(num_layers):\n                hs = hidden_states[layer_idx].cpu().float().numpy()  # (batch, seq_len, hidden)\n\n                for b in range(hs.shape[0]):\n                    if attention_mask is not None:\n                        mask = attention_mask[b].cpu().numpy()\n                        seq_len = int(mask.sum())\n                    else:\n                        seq_len = hs.shape[1]\n\n                    # First token\n                    all_activations['first'][layer_idx].append(hs[b, 0, :])\n\n                    # Last token (last non-padding token)\n                    all_activations['last'][layer_idx].append(hs[b, seq_len-1, :])\n\n                    # Mean pooling (over non-padding tokens)\n                    all_activations['mean'][layer_idx].append(hs[b, :seq_len, :].mean(axis=0))\n\n                    # Max pooling (over non-padding tokens)\n                    all_activations['max'][layer_idx].append(hs[b, :seq_len, :].max(axis=0))\n\n            if (i + batch_size) % 100 == 0 or i + batch_size >= len(texts):\n                print(f\"  Extracted {min(i+batch_size, len(texts))}/{len(texts)}\")\n\n    # Convert to numpy arrays\n    for agg in all_activations:\n        for layer_idx in range(num_layers):\n            all_activations[agg][layer_idx] = np.array(all_activations[agg][layer_idx])\n\n    return all_activations\n\ndef train_probe_cv(X, y, n_folds=5, C=1.0):\n    \"\"\"Train a logistic regression probe with cross-validation.\"\"\"\n    skf = StratifiedKFold(n_splits=n_folds, shuffle=True, random_state=42)\n\n    accuracies = []\n    precisions = []\n    recalls = []\n    f1s = []\n    aucs = []\n\n    for fold, (train_idx, val_idx) in enumerate(skf.split(X, y)):\n        X_train, X_val = X[train_idx], X[val_idx]\n        y_train, y_val = y[train_idx], y[val_idx]\n\n        scaler = StandardScaler()\n        X_train_s = scaler.fit_transform(X_train)\n        X_val_s = scaler.transform(X_val)\n\n        probe = LogisticRegression(C=C, max_iter=1000, random_state=42, solver='lbfgs')\n        probe.fit(X_train_s, y_train)\n\n        y_pred = probe.predict(X_val_s)\n        y_proba = probe.predict_proba(X_val_s)[:, 1]\n\n        accuracies.append(accuracy_score(y_val, y_pred))\n        p, r, f, _ = precision_recall_fscore_support(y_val, y_pred, average='binary', zero_division=0)\n        precisions.append(p)\n        recalls.append(r)\n        f1s.append(f)\n        try:\n            aucs.append(roc_auc_score(y_val, y_proba))\n        except:\n            aucs.append(0.5)\n\n    return {\n        'accuracy': np.mean(accuracies),\n        'accuracy_std': np.std(accuracies),\n        'precision': np.mean(precisions),\n        'recall': np.mean(recalls),\n        'f1': np.mean(f1s),\n        'roc_auc': np.mean(aucs),\n        'roc_auc_std': np.std(aucs),\n    }\n\ndef main():\n    start_time = time.time()\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n    print(\"Truth Analysis Probing Pipeline\")\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n\n    # Load data\n    print(\"\\n1. Loading behavioral labels...\")\n    texts, labels = load_behavioral_labels()\n    print(f\"   Loaded {len(texts)} examples\")\n    print(f\"   Label distribution: {np.sum(labels==1)} correct (1), {np.sum(labels==0)} incorrect (0)\")\n    print(f\"   Baseline accuracy (majority class): {max(np.mean(labels), 1-np.mean(labels)):.3f}\")\n\n    # Load model\n    print(\"\\n2. Loading model...\")\n    model_name = \"HuggingFaceTB/SmolLM2-1.7B\"\n    tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained(model_name)\n    model = AutoModel.from_pretrained(model_name, torch_dtype=torch.float16)\n\n    if tokenizer.pad_token is None:\n        tokenizer.pad_token = tokenizer.eos_token\n\n    if torch.cuda.is_available():\n        model = model.cuda()\n    model.eval()\n\n    num_layers = model.config.num_hidden_layers + 1\n    print(f\"   Model loaded: {num_layers} layers (including embedding), hidden_size={model.config.hidden_size}\")\n\n    # Extract activations\n    print(\"\\n3. Extracting activations from all layers...\")\n    activations = extract_all_activations(model, tokenizer, texts, batch_size=8)\n    print(f\"   Done! Shape check - layer 0, mean: {activations['mean'][0].shape}\")\n\n    # Free model memory\n    del model\n    torch.cuda.empty_cache()\n\n    # Train probes\n    print(\"\\n4. Training probes across all layers and aggregation strategies...\")\n    aggregation_methods = ['first', 'last', 'mean', 'max']\n    results = {}\n\n    best_score = -1\n    best_config = None\n    best_X = None\n\n    for agg in aggregation_methods:\n        results[agg] = []\n        print(f\"\\n   --- Aggregation: {agg} ---\")\n        for layer_idx in range(num_layers):\n            X = activations[agg][layer_idx]\n            metrics = train_probe_cv(X, labels, n_folds=5)\n            metrics['layer'] = layer_idx\n            metrics['aggregation'] = agg\n            results[agg].append(metrics)\n\n            if metrics['roc_auc'] > best_score:\n                best_score = metrics['roc_auc']\n                best_config = (agg, layer_idx)\n                best_X = X.copy()\n\n            if layer_idx % 6 == 0 or layer_idx == num_layers - 1:\n                print(f\"   Layer {layer_idx:2d}: Acc={metrics['accuracy']:.3f} (±{metrics['accuracy_std']:.3f}), \"\n                      f\"F1={metrics['f1']:.3f}, AUC={metrics['roc_auc']:.3f} (±{metrics['roc_auc_std']:.3f})\")\n\n    print(f\"\\n   Best config: {best_config[0]} aggregation, layer {best_config[1]} \"\n          f\"(AUC={best_score:.3f})\")\n\n    # Train final probe on best config\n    print(\"\\n5. Training final probe on best configuration...\")\n    best_agg, best_layer = best_config\n\n    scaler = StandardScaler()\n    X_scaled = scaler.fit_transform(best_X)\n\n    # Try different regularization strengths\n    best_C = 1.0\n    best_C_score = -1\n    for C in [0.01, 0.1, 1.0, 10.0]:\n        cv_metrics = train_probe_cv(best_X, labels, n_folds=5, C=C)\n        print(f\"   C={C}: AUC={cv_metrics['roc_auc']:.3f}, Acc={cv_metrics['accuracy']:.3f}\")\n        if cv_metrics['roc_auc'] > best_C_score:\n            best_C_score = cv_metrics['roc_auc']\n            best_C = C\n\n    print(f\"   Best C: {best_C} (AUC={best_C_score:.3f})\")\n\n    # Train final model on all data\n    final_probe = LogisticRegression(C=best_C, max_iter=1000, random_state=42, solver='lbfgs')\n    final_probe.fit(X_scaled, labels)\n\n    # Save probe\n    os.makedirs(\"final_probe\", exist_ok=True)\n    probe_data = {\n        'model': final_probe,\n        'scaler': scaler,\n        'layer': best_layer,\n        'aggregation': best_agg,\n        'C': best_C,\n        'num_layers': num_layers,\n        'hidden_size': best_X.shape[1],\n    }\n    with open(\"final_probe/probe.pkl\", \"wb\") as f:\n        pickle.dump(probe_data, f)\n    print(f\"   Saved probe to final_probe/probe.pkl\")\n\n    # Get final metrics via cross-validation\n    final_cv_metrics = train_probe_cv(best_X, labels, n_folds=5, C=best_C)\n\n    # Also compute full-data metrics\n    y_pred_full = final_probe.predict(X_scaled)\n    y_proba_full = final_probe.predict_proba(X_scaled)[:, 1]\n    full_acc = accuracy_score(labels, y_pred_full)\n    full_p, full_r, full_f1, _ = precision_recall_fscore_support(labels, y_pred_full, average='binary')\n    full_auc = roc_auc_score(labels, y_proba_full)\n\n    metrics_output = {\n        'best_layer': int(best_layer),\n        'best_aggregation': best_agg,\n        'best_C': float(best_C),\n        'cv_accuracy': float(final_cv_metrics['accuracy']),\n        'cv_accuracy_std': float(final_cv_metrics['accuracy_std']),\n        'cv_precision': float(final_cv_metrics['precision']),\n        'cv_recall': float(final_cv_metrics['recall']),\n        'cv_f1': float(final_cv_metrics['f1']),\n        'cv_roc_auc': float(final_cv_metrics['roc_auc']),\n        'cv_roc_auc_std': float(final_cv_metrics['roc_auc_std']),\n        'train_accuracy': float(full_acc),\n        'train_precision': float(full_p),\n        'train_recall': float(full_r),\n        'train_f1': float(full_f1),\n        'train_roc_auc': float(full_auc),\n        'num_examples': int(len(labels)),\n        'num_positive': int(np.sum(labels == 1)),\n        'num_negative': int(np.sum(labels == 0)),\n        'baseline_accuracy': float(max(np.mean(labels), 1 - np.mean(labels))),\n    }\n\n    with open(\"metrics.json\", \"w\") as f:\n        json.dump(metrics_output, f, indent=2)\n    print(f\"   Saved metrics to metrics.json\")\n\n    # 6. Generate Visualizations\n    print(\"\\n6. Generating visualizations...\")\n\n    # Plot 1: Probe accuracy across layers for all aggregation methods\n    fig, axes = plt.subplots(2, 2, figsize=(14, 10))\n\n    # Accuracy across layers\n    ax = axes[0, 0]\n    for agg in aggregation_methods:\n        layers = [r['layer'] for r in results[agg]]\n        accs = [r['accuracy'] for r in results[agg]]\n        ax.plot(layers, accs, marker='o', label=agg, linewidth=2, markersize=4)\n    ax.axhline(y=max(np.mean(labels), 1-np.mean(labels)), color='gray', linestyle='--', label='baseline', alpha=0.7)\n    ax.set_xlabel('Layer')\n    ax.set_ylabel('Accuracy')\n    ax.set_title('Probe Accuracy Across Layers')\n    ax.legend()\n    ax.grid(True, alpha=0.3)\n\n    # ROC-AUC across layers\n    ax = axes[0, 1]\n    for agg in aggregation_methods:\n        layers = [r['layer'] for r in results[agg]]\n        aucs = [r['roc_auc'] for r in results[agg]]\n        ax.plot(layers, aucs, marker='o', label=agg, linewidth=2, markersize=4)\n    ax.axhline(y=0.5, color='gray', linestyle='--', label='chance', alpha=0.7)\n    ax.set_xlabel('Layer')\n    ax.set_ylabel('ROC-AUC')\n    ax.set_title('Probe ROC-AUC Across Layers')\n    ax.legend()\n    ax.grid(True, alpha=0.3)\n\n    # F1 across layers\n    ax = axes[1, 0]\n    for agg in aggregation_methods:\n        layers = [r['layer'] for r in results[agg]]\n        f1s = [r['f1'] for r in results[agg]]\n        ax.plot(layers, f1s, marker='o', label=agg, linewidth=2, markersize=4)\n    ax.set_xlabel('Layer')\n    ax.set_ylabel('F1 Score')\n    ax.set_title('Probe F1 Score Across Layers')\n    ax.legend()\n    ax.grid(True, alpha=0.3)\n\n    # Best aggregation comparison (bar chart)\n    ax = axes[1, 1]\n    best_auc_per_agg = {}\n    for agg in aggregation_methods:\n        aucs = [r['roc_auc'] for r in results[agg]]\n        best_idx = np.argmax(aucs)\n        best_auc_per_agg[agg] = {\n            'auc': aucs[best_idx],\n            'layer': best_idx,\n            'acc': results[agg][best_idx]['accuracy'],\n            'f1': results[agg][best_idx]['f1'],\n        }\n\n    x_pos = range(len(aggregation_methods))\n    bars_auc = [best_auc_per_agg[agg]['auc'] for agg in aggregation_methods]\n    bars_acc = [best_auc_per_agg[agg]['acc'] for agg in aggregation_methods]\n    bars_f1 = [best_auc_per_agg[agg]['f1'] for agg in aggregation_methods]\n\n    width = 0.25\n    ax.bar([x - width for x in x_pos], bars_auc, width, label='ROC-AUC', alpha=0.8)\n    ax.bar(list(x_pos), bars_acc, width, label='Accuracy', alpha=0.8)\n    ax.bar([x + width for x in x_pos], bars_f1, width, label='F1', alpha=0.8)\n    ax.set_xticks(list(x_pos))\n    labels_agg = [f\"{agg}\\n(L{best_auc_per_agg[agg]['layer']})\" for agg in aggregation_methods]\n    ax.set_xticklabels(labels_agg)\n    ax.set_ylabel('Score')\n    ax.set_title('Best Performance per Aggregation Strategy')\n    ax.legend()\n    ax.grid(True, alpha=0.3, axis='y')\n\n    plt.suptitle('Truth Analysis Probing: SmolLM2-1.7B on TruthfulQA', fontsize=14, fontweight='bold')\n    plt.tight_layout()\n    plt.savefig('probe_performance_layers.png', dpi=150, bbox_inches='tight')\n    plt.close()\n    print(\"   Saved probe_performance_layers.png\")\n\n    # Plot 2: Heatmap of AUC across layers and aggregations\n    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(10, 6))\n    auc_matrix = np.zeros((len(aggregation_methods), num_layers))\n    for i, agg in enumerate(aggregation_methods):\n        for j in range(num_layers):\n            auc_matrix[i, j] = results[agg][j]['roc_auc']\n\n    im = ax.imshow(auc_matrix, aspect='auto', cmap='YlOrRd', interpolation='nearest')\n    ax.set_yticks(range(len(aggregation_methods)))\n    ax.set_yticklabels(aggregation_methods)\n    ax.set_xlabel('Layer')\n    ax.set_ylabel('Aggregation')\n    ax.set_title('ROC-AUC Heatmap: Layer x Aggregation')\n    plt.colorbar(im, ax=ax, label='ROC-AUC')\n\n    # Annotate\n    for i in range(len(aggregation_methods)):\n        for j in range(num_layers):\n            val = auc_matrix[i, j]\n            color = 'white' if val > 0.6 else 'black'\n            ax.text(j, i, f'{val:.2f}', ha='center', va='center', fontsize=6, color=color)\n\n    plt.tight_layout()\n    plt.savefig('probe_heatmap.png', dpi=150, bbox_inches='tight')\n    plt.close()\n    print(\"   Saved probe_heatmap.png\")\n\n    # Plot 3: Accuracy with error bars for best aggregation\n    fig, ax = plt.subplots(figsize=(10, 5))\n    layers = range(num_layers)\n    accs = [results[best_agg][l]['accuracy'] for l in layers]\n    stds = [results[best_agg][l]['accuracy_std'] for l in layers]\n    aucs_best = [results[best_agg][l]['roc_auc'] for l in layers]\n    auc_stds = [results[best_agg][l]['roc_auc_std'] for l in layers]\n\n    ax.errorbar(list(layers), accs, yerr=stds, marker='o', linewidth=2, markersize=5,\n                capsize=3, label=f'Accuracy ({best_agg})', color='tab:blue')\n    ax.errorbar(list(layers), aucs_best, yerr=auc_stds, marker='s', linewidth=2, markersize=5,\n                capsize=3, label=f'ROC-AUC ({best_agg})', color='tab:red')\n    ax.axhline(y=max(np.mean(labels), 1-np.mean(labels)), color='gray', linestyle='--',\n               label='Baseline accuracy', alpha=0.7)\n    ax.axhline(y=0.5, color='lightgray', linestyle=':', label='Chance AUC', alpha=0.7)\n    ax.set_xlabel('Layer')\n    ax.set_ylabel('Score')\n    ax.set_title(f'Probe Performance with Confidence (Best Aggregation: {best_agg})')\n    ax.legend()\n    ax.grid(True, alpha=0.3)\n    plt.tight_layout()\n    plt.savefig('probe_confidence.png', dpi=150, bbox_inches='tight')\n    plt.close()\n    print(\"   Saved probe_confidence.png\")\n\n    # extract_all_activations(model, tokenizer, texts, batch_size=16):\n    \"\"\"Extract activations from ALL layers.\"\"\"\n    model.eval()\n    device = next(model.parameters()).device\n    num_layers = model.config.num_hidden_layers + 1\n\n    all_activations = {\n        'first': [[] for _ in range(num_layers)],\n        'last': [[] for _ in range(num_layers)],\n        'mean': [[] for _ in        else:\n                        seq_len = hs.shape[1]\n                    all_activations['first'][layer_idx].append(hs[b, 0, :])\n                    all_activations['last'][layer_idx].append(hs[b, seq_len-1, :])\n                    all_activations['mean'][layer_idx].append(hs[b, :seq_len, :].mean(axis=0))\n                    all_activations['max'][layer_idx].append(hs[b, :seq_len, :].max(axis=0))\n\n            if (i + batch_size) % 200 == 0:\n                print(f\"  Extracted {min(i+batch_size, len(texts))}/{len(texts)}\")\n\n    for agg in all_activations:\n        for layer_idx in range(num_layers):\n            all_activations[agg][layer_idx] = np.array(all_activations[agg][layer_idx])\n\n    return all_activations\n\ndef train_probe_cv(X, y, n_folds=5, C=1.0, class_weight='balanced'):\n    \"\"\"Train probe with class weighting and   for fold, (train_idx, val_idx) in enumerate(skf.split(X, y)):\n        X_train, X_val = X[train_idx], X[val_idx]\n        y_train, y_val = y[train_idx], y[val_idx]\n\n        scaler = StandardScaler()\n        X_train_s = scaler.fit_transform(X_train)\n        X_val_s = scaler.transform(X_val)\n\n        probe = LogisticRegression(C=C, max_iter=1000, random_state=42,\n                                   solver='lbfgs', class_weight=class_weight)\n        probe.fit(X_train_s, y_train)\n\n        y_pred = probe.predict(X_val_s)\n        y_proba = probe.predict_proba(X_val_s)[:, 1]\n\n        metrics_lists['accuracy'].append(accuracy_score(y_val, y_pred))\n        p, r, f, _ = precision_recall_fscore_support(y_val, y_pred, average='binary', zero_division=0)\n        metrics_lists['precision'].append(p)\n        metrics_lists['recall'].append(r)\n        metrics_lists['f1'].append(f)\n        try:\n            metrics_lists['roc_auc'].append(roc_auc_score(y_val, y_proba))\n        except:\n            metrics_lists['roc_auc'].append(0.5)\n\n    return {k: np.mean(v) for k, v in metrics_lists.items()} | \\\n           {f'{k}_std': np.std(v) for k, v in metrics_lists.items()}\n\ndef main():\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n    print(\"Improved Probing Pipeline\")\n    print(\"=\" * 60)\n\n    # Load data\n    texts, labels = load_behavioral_labels()\n best_X = None\n\n    for agg in aggregation_methods:\n        results[agg] = []\n        for layer_idx in range(num_layers):\n            X = activations[agg][layer_idx]\n            metrics =          if metrics['roc_auc'] > best_score:\n                best_score = metrics['roc_auc']\n                best_config = (agg, layer_idx)\n                best_X = X.copy()\n\n        # Print best AUC={best_score:.3f}\")\n\n    # Also try multi-layer concatenation for top configurations\n    print(\"\\nTrying multi-layer concatenation...\")\n    top_layers_mean = sorted(range(num_layers),\n python3\n\"\"\"\nImproved probing with class-weighted logistic regression and multi-layer combinations.\nFocuses on the best configurations identified in the initial sweep.\n\"\"\"\nimport json\nimport pickle\nimport os\nimport numpy as np\nimport torch\nfrom transformers import AutoModel, AutoTokenizer\nfrom sklearn.linear_model import LogisticRegression\nfrom sklearn.model_selection import StratifiedKFold\nfrom sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler\nfrom sklearn.metrics import (\n    accuracy_score, precision_recall_fscore_support,\n    roc_auc_score\n)\nimport matplotlib\nmatplotlib.use('Agg')\nimport matplotlib.pyplot as plt\n\ndef load_behavioral_labels(filepath=\"behavioral_labels.jsonl\"):\n    texts, labels = [], []\n    with open(filepath, 'r') as f:\n        for line in f:\n            item = json.loads(line)\n            texts.append(item['text'])\n            labels.append(item['label'])\n    return texts, np.array(labels)\n\ndef extract_all_activations(model, tokenizer, texts, batch_size=16):\n    \"\"\"Extract activations from ALL layers.\"\"\"\n    model.eval()\n    device = next(model.parameters()).device\n    num_layers = model.config.num_hidden_layers + 1\n\n    all_activations = {\n        'first': [[] for _ in range(num_layers)],\n        'last': [[] for _ in range(num_layers)],\n        'mean': [[] for _ in range(num_layers)],\n        'max': [[] for _ in range(num_layers)],\n    }\n\n    with torch.no_grad():\n        for i in range(0, len(texts), batch_size):\n            batch_texts = texts[i:i+batch_size]\n            inputs = tokenizer(\n                batch_texts, return_tensors=\"pt\",\n                truncation=True, max_length=512, padding=True\n            )\n            inputs = {k: v.to(device) for k, v in inputs.items()}\n            outputs = model(**inputs, output_hidden_states=True)\n            hidden_states = outputs.hidden_states\n            attention_mask = inputs.get('attention_mask', None)\n\n            for layer_idx in range(num_layers):\n                hs = hidden_states[layer_idx].cpu().float().numpy()\n                for b in range(hs.shape[0]):\n                    if attention_mask is not None:\n                        mask = attention_mask[b].cpu().numpy()\n                        seq_len = int(mask.sum())\n                    else:\n                        seq_len = hs.shape[1]\n                    all_activations['first'][layer_idx].append(hs[b, 0, :])\n                    all_activations['last'][layer_idx].append(hs[b, seq_len-1, :])\n                    all_activations['mean'][layer_idx].append(hs[b, :seq_len, :].mean(axis=0))\n                    all_activations['max'][layer_idx].append(hs[b, :seq_len, :].max(axis=0))\n\n            if (i + batch_size) % 200 == 0:\n                print(f\"  Extracted {min(i+batch_size, len(texts))}/{len(texts)}\")\n\n    for agg in all_activations:\n        for layer_idx in range(num_layers):\n            all_activations[agg][layer_idx] = np.array(all_activations[agg][layer_idx])\n\n    return all_activations\n\ndef train_probe_cv(X, y, n_folds=5, C=1.0, class_weight='balanced'):\n    \"\"\"Train probe with class weighting and cross-validation.\"\"\"\n    skf = StratifiedKFold(n_splits=n_folds, shuffle=True, random_state=42)\n\n    metrics_lists = {'accuracy': [], 'precision': [], 'recall': [], 'f1': [], 'roc_auc': []}\n\n    for fold, (train_idx, val_idx) in enumerate(skf.split(X, y)):\n        X_train, X_val = X[train_idx], X[val_idx]\n        y_train, y_val = y[train_idx], y[val_idx]\n\n        scaler = StandardScaler()\n        X_train_s = scaler.fit_transform(X_train)\n        X_val_s = scaler.transform(X_val)\n\n        probe = LogisticRegression(C=C, max_iter=1000, random_state=42,\n                                   solver='lbfgs', class_weight=class_weight)\n        probe.fit(X_train_s, y_train)\n\n        y_pred = probe.predict(X_val_s)\n        y_proba = probe.predict_proba(X_val_s)[:, metrics_lists['precision'].append(p)\n        metrics_lists['recall'].append(r)\n        metrics_lists['f1'].append(f)\n        try:\n            metrics_lists['roc_auc'].append(roc_auc_score(y_val, y_proba))\n        except:\n            metrics_lists['roc_auc'].append(0.5)\n\n    return {k: np.mean(v) for k, v in metrics_lists.items()} | \\\n           {f'{k}_std': np.std(v) for k, v in [2026-06-10 11:55:32 UTC] {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-opus-4-6","id":"msg_019cGm8HXNbwMygEBVyWzbyV","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_015LsMiPkwCPkgv4vJsNmcUP","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/iopsstor/scratch/cscs/oyasunaga/autointerp_runs/jobs/truth_analysis_HuggingFaceTB_SmolLM2-1.7B_2513490/analysis.md","content":"# Truth Analysis Probing: SmolLM2-1.7B on TruthfulQA\n\n## Overview\n\nThis analysis investigates whether SmolLM2-1.7B internally represents its own truthfulness — specifically, whether linear probes on the model's hidden states can predict whether the model will answer a question correctly or incorrectly.\n\n## Methodology\n\n### 1. Behavioral Labeling\n\nWe ran SmolLM2-1.7B on 817 TruthfulQA questions using greedy decoding (temperature=1.0, do_sample=False) with a simple \"Q: {question}\\nA:\" prompt format. Each model response was compared against the provided `correct_answers` list using a multi-strategy matching approach:\n\n- **Sentiment checking**: Detecting yes/no mismatches between model response and correct answer\n- **Direct containment**: Checking if the correct answer is contained in the response (or vice versa)\n- **Synonym expansion**: Handling common abbreviations (US/United States, UK/United Kingdom)\n- **Key word overlap**: Computing overlap ratio of content words (threshold: 60%)\n\n**Results**: The model answered 173/817 questions correctly (21.2%), reflecting the intentional difficulty of TruthfulQA which tests common misconceptions.\n\n### 2. Activation Extraction\n\nWe extracted hidden state activations from all 25 layers (embedding + 24 transformer layers) of the model, using four token aggregation strategies:\n- **First token**: First token representation\n- **Last token**: Last non-padding token representation\n- **Mean pooling**: Average across all non-padding tokens\n- **Max pooling**: Element-wise maximum across non-padding tokens\n\n### 3. Probe Training\n\nLinear probes (logistic regression with balanced class weights) were trained with 5-fold stratified cross-validation across all 100 layer×aggregation combinations.\n\n## Key Findings\n\n### 1. Which layers best predict correctness?\n\n| Aggregation | Best Layer | ROC-AUC | Accuracy | F1 |\n|------------|-----------|---------|----------|------|\n| **Mean** | **Layer 9** | **0.661** | **0.721** | **0.308** |\n| Last | Layer 23 | 0.645 | 0.725 | 0.299 |\n| Max | Layer 22 | 0.617 | 0.730 | 0.250 |\n| First | Layer 0 | 0.548 | 0.661 | 0.342 |\n\n**Layer 9 (middle of the network) with mean pooling is the most informative**, achieving the highest ROC-AUC of 0.661. This is notable — it suggests that **mid-layer representations** encode the most information about whether the model will produce a correct response. This aligns with research suggesting that factual knowledge is primarily encoded in middle transformer layers.\n\nThe **last-token aggregation peaks at the final layers** (L23, L22), which makes sense as these layers prepare the actual output. The last-token approach captures the model's \"decision state\" right before generation.\n\n### 2. Which token positions are most informative?\n\n**Mean pooling > Last token > Max pooling >> First token**\n\n- **Mean pooling** (best AUC: 0.661): Provides the most robust signal by averaging across all token positions, capturing global question understanding.\n- **Last token** (best AUC: 0.645): Second-best, captures the model's final \"summary\" representation used for next-token prediction.\n- **Max pooling** (best AUC: 0.617): Captures the strongest individual feature activations but adds noise.\n- **First token** (best AUC: 0.548): Near-chance performance. The first token position encodes little about the model's knowledge of the answer, as it hasn't processed the full question.\n\n### 3. Does the model internally \"know\" when it's about to give a wrong answer?\n\n**Partially, but weakly.** The probe achieves ROC-AUC of 0.661 (above 0.5 chance), indicating that the model's internal representations do contain some signal about whether it will answer correctly. However, the signal is modest:\n\n- The CV accuracy (0.721) is actually **below** the baseline (0.788, predicting all-incorrect), meaning the probe sacrifices some accuracy on the majority class to gain recall on the minority class.\n- With balanced class weights, recall reaches 0.295 (the probe correctly identifies ~30% of the questions the model gets right).\n- The signal is distributed across layers, with a peak in the middle layers.\n\n**Interpretation**: SmolLM2-1.7B has a weak internal signal for truthfulness. The model partially \"knows\" the difference between questions it can answer correctly vs. those where it will produce misconceptions, but this signal is not strong enough for reliable self-monitoring. This suggests:\n\n1. The model's factual knowledge (layers 8-10) provides some discriminative signal\n2. The model lacks a robust \"confidence calibration\" mechanism\n3. The relatively small model size (1.7B parameters) likely limits the complexity of internal self-monitoring\n\n### 4. Multi-layer Analysis\n\nConcatenating activations from multiple layers slightly improves performance:\n- Mean layers [9, 10, 23] concatenated: AUC = 0.674\n- Last layers [23, 8] concatenated: AUC = 0.669\n\nThis suggests that different layers capture complementary aspects of truthfulness.\n\n## Probe Configuration\n\n- **Final probe**: Logistic Regression with balanced class weights\n- **Layer**: 9 (mean aggregation)\n- **Regularization**: C=0.01\n- **Features**: 2048-dimensional hidden state vectors\n- **Preprocessing**: StandardScaler normalization\n\n## Metrics Summary\n\n| Metric | Value |\n|--------|-------|\n| CV ROC-AUC | 0.661 ± 0.064 |\n| CV Accuracy | 0.721 ± 0.033 |\n| CV Precision | 0.338 |\n| CV Recall | 0.295 |\n| CV F1 | 0.308 |\n| Baseline (majority class) | 0.788 |\n| Label distribution | 173 correct / 644 incorrect |\n\n## Visualizations\n\n1. **probe_performance_layers.png**: Accuracy, ROC-AUC, F1, and Recall across all layers for each aggregation strategy\n2. **probe_heatmap.png**: Full heatmap of ROC-AUC across layers × aggregation methods\n3. **probe_confidence.png**: Performance with error bars for the best aggregation method\n4. **truthfulness_knowledge.png**: Area chart showing where the model \"knows\" it's right/wrong\n\n## Conclusions\n\n1. SmolLM2-1.7B has a **weak but above-chance internal representation of its own truthfulness** (AUC=0.661 vs. chance=0.5).\n2. **Middle layers (8-10)** are most informative when using mean-pooled representations, suggesting factual knowledge is encoded there.\n3. **Last layers (22-23)** are most informative when using last-token representations, reflecting the model's output preparation.\n4. The model lacks a strong \"self-knowledge\" signal, which is expected for a relatively small language model without RLHF or instruction tuning.\n5. **Mean pooling outperforms all other aggregation strategies**, suggesting that truthfulness is a distributed property of the full representation rather than concentrated at specific token positions.\n\n## Files\n\n- `behavioral_labels.jsonl` — Model-evaluated labels (173 correct, 644 incorrect)\n- `final_probe/probe.pkl` — Best trained probe (Layer 9, mean, balanced LR)\n- `metrics.json` — Quantitative metrics\n- `all_probe_results.json` — Full results across all layers and aggregation methods\n- `probe_performance_layers.png` — Multi-panel performance visualization\n- `probe_heatmap.png` — AUC heatmap\n- `probe_confidence.png` — Performance with error bars\n- `truthfulness_knowledge.png` — Knowledge pattern visualization\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"stop_details":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":555,"cache_read_input_tokens":66124,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":555,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":2062,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"global"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"f0cda53f-9198-46c2-b0ae-9e4a0de1b490","uuid":"bd90bace-eef3-4145-a528-5d346f132340"}
